    This is reminiscent of when during WWI the Allies switched from cloth caps to steel helmets. They were surprised that the number of head injuries actually increased, until it was pointed out that with the cloth caps, those same injuries would've been fatalities.

    This is why you can’t have science without understanding cognitive biases and logical fallacies. I wish US public schools would spend time exploring these examples because it’s usually still based on rote memorization or process, not on how to challenge and analyze.
